[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis of Code Snippets in Relation to Evaluation Report[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Core Insights Extracted[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Security Validation Pattern**: The patch correctly implements three-layer [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnull byte check, absolute path rejection, directory boundary [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mverification[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m as evidenced by similar patterns in `FileSystemFetcher` and `FSUtil`.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Error Handling Gap**: The critical issue is that the patch throws [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`IOException` for validation failures, which propagates through the `[0m[1;35mmain[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethod's `throws IOException` clause, causing the process to exit with error status[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m77[0m[39m. The fuzzer interprets this as a crash.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Tika's Error Recovery Patterns**: Multiple code snippets [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`PackageParser`, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`BundleIT`, `PDFParserConfig`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m demonstrate that Tika parsers handle intermediate [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfailures gracefully by:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Catching exceptions during individual entry/file processing[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Logging/recording errors without stopping overall processing[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Using `continue` to skip problematic entries[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Only propagating critical exceptions that prevent overall operation[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **The Malicious Test Case**: The evaluation report shows the fuzzer uses a tar [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marchive with a path traversal entry [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`..[0m[35m/../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The expected [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior should be:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Skip the malicious entry with a warning[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Continue processing any other valid entries[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Exit with success status [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m if the tar file itself is readable[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause Identified[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe patch successfully blocks the security vulnerability but fails to handle the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidation failure gracefully. The root cause is **missing try-catch block around [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindividual entry processing**, causing validation IOExceptions to terminate the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentire extraction process.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Critical Logic to Preserve[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The three-layer security validation from the patch must be retained[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The loop structure that processes entries sequentially must continue[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The tar file reading mechanism must remain unchanged[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Valid entries must still be extracted successfully[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Comprehensive Fix Strategy[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Strategy Overview[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mModify `TikaUntar.java` to wrap individual entry processing in a try-catch block [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat catches IOExceptions thrown during validation, logs warnings to System.err, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand continues processing the next entry. This maintains the security fix while [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallowing graceful degradation for malicious entries.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Implementation Steps[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Retain all three validation checks from the previous patch:**[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Null byte detection in entry name[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Absolute path rejection[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Directory boundary verification using [0m[1;35mnormalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and [0m[1;35mstartsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Wrap the entry processing block [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m42[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m48[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in a try-catch block:**[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Place try immediately after `if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtae.isFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m`[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Catch `IOException` specifically for validation failures and other entry-level[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39merrors[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add a catch block that logs the error to `System.err` with the entry name and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39merror message[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Use `continue` to skip to the next entry after logging[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Adjust the loop flow:**[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Move `tae = [0m[1;35mtais.getNextEntry[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` call outside the try-catch to ensure it's [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malways executed[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensure the loop continues even after catching exceptions[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Preserve the main method signature:**[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Keep `throws IOException` in the main method signature[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This ensures tar file reading errors [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., corrupt tar file, file not found[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstill propagate[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Only entry-level validation failures are caught and handled gracefully[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Detailed Patch Structure[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: `tika-app/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/cli/TikaUntar.java`[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Changes to lines [0m[1;36m41[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m50[0m[39m:**[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhile [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtae != null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtae.isFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            Path target = [0m[1;35mextractDir.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Validation [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Check for null bytes[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.contains[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"\u0000"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Invalid entry name contains null byte: "[0m[39m + [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Validation [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Check for absolute paths[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            Path entryPath = [0m[1;35mPaths.get[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mentryPath.isAbsolute[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Cannot extract entry with absolute path: "[0m[39m +[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Validation [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Validate descendant relationship[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            Path normalizedExtractDir = [0m[1;35mextractDir.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            Path normalizedTarget = [0m[1;35mtarget.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mnormalizedTarget.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnormalizedExtractDir[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Entry is outside of the extraction [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mdirectory: "[0m[39m + [0m[1;35mtae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mFiles.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                [0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mFiles.write[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtarget, [0m[1;35mtais.readAllBytes[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIOException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Log warning about invalid entry and continue processing[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mSystem.err.println[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Skipping entry '"[0m[39m + [0m[1;35mtae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m + [0m[32m"': "[0m[39m + [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35me.getMessage[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    tae = [0m[1;35mtais.getNextEntry[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Justification[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why this is the optimal approach:**[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Maintains Security**: All three validation layers from the previous patch are [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreserved, preventing path traversal attacks[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Follows Tika Patterns**: Mirrors the error handling approach used in [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mPackageParser.parseEntries[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `BundleIT`, which catch intermediate exceptions [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand continue processing[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Satisfies Fuzzer Requirements**: The process exits with status [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m for archives [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontaining malicious entries, as the fuzzer expects graceful handling of invalid [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minput[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Minimal Changes**: Only adds try-catch and error logging, preserving all [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting functionality[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**How it preserves existing logic:**[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The tar reading loop structure remains unchanged[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Valid entries are still extracted exactly as before[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Directory creation and file writing logic is untouched[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. The main method's IOException handling for tar file errors is preserved[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**How it addresses the evaluation report issues:**[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Initial Issue [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath Traversal[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: The three validation checks block the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Additional Issue [0m[1;39m([0m[39mFuzzer Crash[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: The try-catch prevents validation [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIOExceptions from propagating, allowing graceful continuation[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **DEDUP_TOKEN Change**: The different crash signature won't occur because no [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexception propagates to the fuzzer harness[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential side effects and mitigation:**[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Silent Failures**: Malicious entries are skipped with only stderr logging[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: The stderr output provides visibility into skipped entries[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Rationale**: This matches Tika's philosophy of [0m[32m"best effort"[0m[39m parsing[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Partial Extraction**: Archives with both valid and invalid entries result in [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpartial extraction[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: This is the intended behavior - extract what's safe[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Rationale**: Aligns with how `PackageParser` handles mixed-validity archives[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **No Entry Count Tracking**: Unlike some parsers, we don't track how many [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentries were skipped[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: Each skipped entry is logged to stderr[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Rationale**: TikaUntar is a simple utility without metadata framework[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Reference to similar solutions:**[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **[0m[1;35mPackageParser.parseEntries[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m368[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m413[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Uses try-catch to continue [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing despite entry-level failures[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **BundleIT** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m328[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m358[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Demonstrates catch-and-continue pattern with [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSystem.err logging[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **PDFParserConfig.catchIntermediateIOExceptions**: Shows Tika's philosophy of [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcatching intermediate exceptions while allowing overall processing to continue[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Testing Considerations[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix should:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Pass existing tests**: `[0m[1;35mTikaUntarTest.testBasic[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` should still pass as valid [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentries are extracted normally[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Handle fuzzer input**: The malicious tar with `..[0m[35m/../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m` should [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomplete without crashing[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Maintain security**: Path traversal attempts should be blocked and logged[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
